mypy: allow-untyped-defs\nr\"\"\"Implementation for gradient noise injection.\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import Callable, Optional\n\nimport torch\nfrom torch.optim.optimizer import Optimizer\n\n__all__ = [\"GradientNoiseInjector\"]\n\n\nclass GradientNoiseInjector:\n    r\"\"\"Wraps an optimizer to inject Gaussian noise into gradients before each step.\n\n    This implements the technique from \"Adding Gradient Noise Improves Learning for\n    Very Deep Networks\" where calibrated noise is added to gradients according to a\n    schedule: sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma, where t is the step count.\n\n    Args:\n        optimizer (Optimizer): the base optimizer to wrap\n        eta (float, optional): noise schedule scale factor (default: 0.01)\n        gamma (float, optional): noise schedule decay exponent (default: 0.55)\n\n    Example:\n        >>> base_optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        >>> optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        >>> for epoch in range(num_epochs):\n        ...     for batch in dataloader:\n        ...         output = model(batch)\n        ...         loss = criterion(output, target)\n        ...         loss.backward()\n        ...         optimizer.step()\n        ...         optimizer.zero_grad()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        optimizer: Optimizer,\n        eta: float = 0.01,\n        gamma: float = 0.55\n    ) -> None:\n        if not isinstance(optimizer, Optimizer):\n            raise TypeError(f\"optimizer must be an Optimizer, got {type(optimizer)}\")\n        if eta < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid eta value: {eta}\")\n        if gamma < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid gamma value: {gamma}\")\n\n        self.optimizer = optimizer\n        self.eta = eta\n        self.gamma = gamma\n        self.t = 0  # step counter\n\n    def step(self, closure: Optional[Callable[[], float]] = None) -> Optional[float]:\n        r\"\"\"Performs a single optimization step with gradient noise injection.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model and\n                returns the loss.\n\n        Returns:\n            The loss if a closure is provided, otherwise None.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Inject noise into gradients\n        self._inject_noise()\n\n        # Call the base optimizer's step\n        result = self.optimizer.step(closure)\n\n        # Increment step counter\n        self.t += 1\n\n        return result\n\n Create some gradients\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y = model(x)\n        loss = y.sum()\n        loss.backward()\n\n        # Verify gradients exist\n        for param in model.parameters():\n            self.assertIsNotNone(param.grad)\n\n        # Zero gradients\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\n\n        # Verify gradients are cleared\n        for param in model.parameters():\n            self.assertIsNone(param.grad)\n\n    def test_state_dict_save_and_load(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that state dict correctly saves and restores step counter.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # Due to noise injection, the parameter updates should differ\n        # This is a probabilistic test, but with non-zero noise it should pass\n        params_differ = False\n        for p1, p2 in zip(model.parameters(), model2.parameters()):\n            if not torch.allclose(p1, p2, atol=1e-6):\n                params_differ = True\n                break\n\n        self.assertTrue(params_differ, \"Parameters should differ due to noise injection\")\n\n    def test_variance_decay_schedule(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that variance follows the schedule: sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        eta = 0.01\n        gamma = 0.55\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=eta, gamma=gamma)\n\n        # Check step counter increments\n        self.assertEqual(optimizer.t, 0)\n\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        for step_num in range(5):\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            y = model(x)\n            loss = y.sum()\n            loss.backward()\n\n            # Before step, check the variance would be calculated correctly\n            expected_variance = eta / ((1.0 + step_num) ** gamma)\n\n            optimizer.step()\n\n            # After step, t should be incremented\n            self.assertEqual(optimizer.t, step_num + 1)\n\n        # Verify final step counter\n        self.assertEqual(optimizer.t, 5)\n\n    def test_wraps_different_optimizers(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that GradientNoiseInjector works with different optimizer types.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n\n        # Test with SGD\n        sgd_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        sgd_wrapper = GradientNoiseInjector(sgd_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        self.assertIsInstance(sgd_wrapper.optimizer, SGD)\n\n        # Reset model\n        for param in model.parameters():\n            param.data.normal_()\n\n        # Test with Adam\n        adam_optimizer = Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)\n        adam_wrapper = GradientNoiseInjector(adam_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        self.assertIsInstance(adam_wrapper.optimizer, Adam)\n\n    def test_zero_grad_delegation(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that zero_grad is properly delegated to base optimizer.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # Create some gradients\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y = model(x)\n        loss = y.sum()\n        loss.backward()\n\n        # Verify gradients exist\n        for param in model.parameters():\n            self.assertIsNotNone(param.grad)\n\n        # Zero gradients\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\n\n        # Verify gradients are cleared\n        for param in model.parameters():\n            self.assertIsNone(param.grad)\n\n    def test_state_dict_save_and_load(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that state dict correctly saves and restores step counter.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # Do some steps\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        for _ in range(3):\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            y = model(x)\n            loss = y.sum()\n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step()\n\n        # Save state\n        state = optimizer.state_dict()\n        self.assertEqual(state[\"_gradient_noise_injector_t\"], 3)\n\n        # Create a new optimizer and load state\n        model2 = self._create_simple_model()\n        for p1, p2 in zip(model.parameters(), model2.parameters()):\n            p2.data.copy_(p1.data)\n\n        base_optimizer2 = SGD(model2.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer2 = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer2, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        optimizer2.load_state_dict(state)\n        self.assertEqual(optimizer2.t, 3)\n\n    def test_invalid_parameters(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that invalid parameters raise appropriate errors.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n\n        # Invalid eta (negative)\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=-0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # Invalid gamma (negative)\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=-0.55)\n\n        # Invalid optimizer\n        with self.assertRaises(TypeError):\n            GradientNoiseInjector(\"not an optimizer\", eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n    def test_with_closure(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that step() works with a closure.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y_target = torch.randn(5, 1)\n\n        def closure():\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            y = model(x)\n            loss = torch.nn.functional.mse_loss(y, y_target)\n            loss.backward()\n            return loss.item()\n\n        # This should not raise an error\n        loss = optimizer.step(closure)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(loss)\n\n    def test_param_groups_access(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that param_groups from base optimizer are accessible.\"\"\"\n        model = self._create_simple_model()\n        base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        # + t)^gamma\n        variance = self.eta / ((1.0 + self.t) ** self.gamma)\n        std = variance ** 0.5\n\n        # Iterate through all parameter groups and parameters\n        for group in self.optimizer.param_groups:\n            for param in group[\"params\"]:\n                if param.grad is not None:\n                    # Add Gaussian noise to gradient\n                    noise = torch.randn_like(param.grad) * std\n                    param.grad.add_(noise)\n\n    def zero_grad(self, set_to_none: bool = False) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Clears the gradients of all optimized :class:`~torch.Tensor` s.\n\n        Args:\n            set_to_none (bool): instead of setting to zero, set the grads to None.\n                This is will in general have lower memory footprint, and improve\n                performance. But it changes certain behaviors. For example:\n                1. When the user tries to access the gradient and performs manual ops\n                on it, a None attribute or a zero tensor will behave differently.\n                2. If the user requests ``zero_grad(set_to_none=True)`` followed by a\n                backward pass, ``.grad``s are guaranteed to be None for params that\n                did not receive a gradient.\n                3. ``torch.optim`` optimizers have a different behavior if the gradient\n                is None versus a zero tensor when the user tries to ``.step()`` without\n                calling ``.zero_grad()``. In order to match zero-gradient behavior of\n                ``torch.optim`` optimizers, set gradient to a zero tensor if\n                ``set_to_none=True`` is not desired. Default: ``False``\n        \"\"\"\n        self.optimizer.zero_grad(set_to_none)\n\n    def state_dict(self) -> dict:\n        r\"\"\"Returns the state of the wrapper as a dict.\n\n        Includes the wrapped optimizer's state plus the step counter.\n        \"\"\"\n        state = self.optimizer.state_dict()\n        state[\"_gradient_noise_injector_t\"] = self.t\n        return state\n\n    def load_state_dict(self, state_dict: dict) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Loads the wrapper state.\n\n        Args:\n            state_dict (dict): state dict as returned by state_dict\n        \"\"\"\n        if \"_gradient_noise_injector_t\" in state_dict:\n            self.t = state_dict.pop(\"_gradient_noise_injector_t\")\n        self.optimizer.load_state_dict(state_dict)\n\n    def __getattr__(self, name: str):\n        r\"\"\"Forward attribute access to the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return object.__getattribute__(self, name)\n        except AttributeError:\n            return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n\n    def __setattr__(self, name: str, value) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Forward attribute setting to the wrapped optimizer if not part of wrapper.\"\"\"\n        # These are the wrapper's own attributes\n        if name in (\"optimizer\", \"eta\", \"gamma\", \"t\"):\n            object.__setattr__(self, name, value)\n        else:\n            # Forward to wrapped optimizer\n            try:\n                setattr(self.optimizer, name, value)\n            except AttributeError:\n                object.__setattr__(self, name, value)\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":138,"oldLines":8,"newStart":138,"newLines":9,"lines":["         if name in (\"optimizer\", \"eta\", \"gamma\", \"t\"):","             object.__setattr__(self, name, value)","         else:","-            #
